## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (deterministic rate laws / ODE kinetics)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is an instantaneous reaction rate expressed as a time-derivative of concentration A(t), which is the standard setting for chemical kinetics modeled by ordinary differential equations. With only {t, A} available, the most likely relationships are empirical or mechanistic rate laws where the consumption/production rate depends on concentration (reaction order, autocatalysis) and possibly explicit time-dependence (e.g., catalyst deactivation, external driving).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order kinetics (constant-rate consumption/production): dA_dt = c0 (e.g., surface-limited regime or constant feed)
- Zero-order decay (constant consumption): dA_dt = -c0 (e.g., reagent consumed at a constant rate)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, pseudo-first-order conditions)
- First-order approach to equilibrium (linear relaxation): dA_dt = c0 * (c1 - A) (relaxation to A_eq = c1)
- Second-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular self-reaction or pseudo-second-order in A)
- General n-th order kinetics (power-law rate law): dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical or fractal-order kinetics)
- Mixed zero+first order (offset + linear): dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A (background source/sink plus first-order term)
- Autocatalytic / logistic-type kinetics in A: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating growth with finite-capacity depletion)
- Gompertz-type autocatalytic kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * log(c1 / A) (sigmoidal-in-time concentration evolution via log-driving force)
- Time-dependent first-order rate constant (linear drift): dA_dt = -(c0 + c1 * t) * A (changing conditions or slow catalyst activation/deactivation)
- Catalyst deactivation / fading activity multiplier: dA_dt = -c0 * A * exp(-c1 * t) (effective rate constant decays in time)
- Diffusion/aging-limited effective rate (hyperbolic in time): dA_dt = -c0 * A / (t + c1) (apparent rate slows as 1/(t+offset) due to transport/aging effects)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If dA_dt keeps a fixed sign and is nearly constant over A, it suggests (signed) zero-order kinetics (dA_dt ≈ ±c0).
- If dA_dt is proportional to A (straight line through origin when plotting dA_dt vs A), it suggests first-order kinetics (dA_dt = -c0*A).
- If dA_dt scales like A**n (curvature in log(-dA_dt) vs log(A)), it suggests n-th order/power-law kinetics (dA_dt = -c0*A**c1).
- A nonzero intercept in dA_dt vs A (dA_dt = c0 + c1*A) indicates an additional constant source/sink term such as feed, background loss, or side reaction.
- If dA_dt changes sign at A = c1 and is linear in (c1 - A), it indicates relaxation toward an equilibrium concentration (dA_dt = c0*(c1 - A)).
- If the magnitude of dA_dt initially increases with A but then decreases after a turning point, it indicates autocatalysis with depletion/limitation (dA_dt = c0*A*(c1 - A)).
- If the apparent first-order rate constant inferred from -(dA_dt/A) varies systematically with time, it suggests explicit time-dependent kinetics such as deactivation: -(dA_dt/A) = c0*exp(-c1*t) or c0 + c1*t.
- If rates slow roughly like 1/(t+offset) at fixed A (or equivalently if -(t+c1)*dA_dt/A is roughly constant), it suggests aging/diffusion-limited or progressively inhibited kinetics (dA_dt = -c0*A/(t+c1)).

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK14)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_p*sin(c4*A)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (for all real t and A in its domain, effectively A≥0 because of sqrt(A)):
\[
f(t,A)= -\alpha \sqrt{A}\;-\;\alpha\,A\,e^{-\beta t}\;+\;\gamma \sin(\delta A)
\]
with \(\alpha=0.1286242133\), \(\beta=0.0593843782\), \(\gamma=0.3894244877\), \(\delta=0.5829315814\).

So any matching candidate must be able (by choosing its free constants) to produce **exactly**:
- a \(\sqrt{A}\) term with a **constant coefficient** (no t-dependence),
- an \(A e^{-\beta t}\) term with **negative exponent in t** and **no other A-dependence** besides the leading \(A\),
- a \(\sin(\delta A)\) term with **no t-dependence** and **no extra wrapping** (not inside exp, not multiplied by exp(t), etc.),
- and **no extra terms** (constants, polynomials, logs, rationals, cos, etc.) unless they can be set to zero.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether those three required structures can be formed and all other structures eliminated.

---

### 1. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3/(A + c4) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*sin(A*c8 + c9))`
Has no `sqrt(A)` term. Also the sine appears only inside an `exp(...)`, not as an additive `sin(δA)`. Cannot match.

### 2. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A**c4*c5 + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)*cos(A*c9)`
No `sqrt(A)` term; trig is `cos` not `sin` and multiplied by `exp(c8 t)`. Cannot match.

### 3. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*sin(A*c7 + c8))`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine only inside exp. Cannot match.

### 4. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4 + c5 + c6*exp(c7*sin(A*c8 + c9))`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine only inside exp. Cannot match.

### 5. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4/(A + c5) + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)*cos(A*c9)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos` with `exp(t)` factor. Cannot match.

### 6. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5*log(1 + c6/A) + c7 + c8*cos(A*c9)`
No `sqrt(A)`. Also trig is `cos`, not `sin`. Cannot match.

### 7. `A**2*c0 + A**2*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5*log(1 + c6/A) + c7 + c8*cos(A*c9)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 8. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4*log(1 + c5/A) + c6 + c7*cos(A*c8)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 9. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*sin(A*c8 + c9))`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine only inside exp. Cannot match.

### 10. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3/(c4 + t) + c5 + c6*exp(c7*sin(A*c8 + c9))`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine only inside exp. Cannot match.

### 11. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*Abs(A) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*sin(A*c7 + c8))`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine only inside exp. Cannot match.

### 12. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + c4 + c5*exp(c6*sin(A*c7 + c8))`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine only inside exp. Cannot match.

### 13. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*sin(A*c6 + c7))`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine only inside exp. Cannot match.

### 14. `sqrt(A)*c0*exp(c1*t) + A**2*c2 + A*c3 + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*log(c8*exp(A*c9) + 1)`
Has a `sqrt(A)` factor but multiplied by `exp(c1 t)`. To match GT, the sqrt term must be independent of t, so we’d need `c1=0`, giving `c0*sqrt(A)` (good in form).
But the candidate has **no additive sin(δA)** term at all. The only A-nonlinearity is `log(1 + c8*exp(A*c9))`, which cannot equal a pure sine for all A. Cannot match.

### 15. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(c3 + t) + A**c4*c5*cos(A*c6) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos` and multiplied by power of A. Cannot match.

### 16. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*cos(A*c3) + A**c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 17. `A*c0 + A*c1/(c2 + t) + A*c3 + A**c4*c5*cos(A*c6) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 18. `A*c0 + A*c1/(c2 + t) + A**c3*c4*cos(A*c5) + c6*Abs(A) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 19. `A*c0 + A*c1/(c2 + t) + A**c3*c4*cos(A*c5) + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 20. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(A + c3) + A*c4/(c5 + t) + A**c6*c7/(A**c6 + c8) + c9`
No `sqrt(A)` and no sine term. Cannot match.

### 21. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A**c3*c4*cos(A*c5) + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 22. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + A**c4*c5*cos(A*c6) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 23. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(A + c3) + A*c4/(c5 + t) + c6 + c7*log(c8*exp(A*c9) + 1)`
No `sqrt(A)` and no sine term. Cannot match.

### 24. `A*c0 + A*c1/(A + c2) + A*c3/(A + c4) + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8 + c9*t) + 1)`
No `sqrt(A)` and no sine term. Cannot match.

### 25. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)*cos(A*c5) + c6*exp(c7*t)*log(c8*t + 1)*cos(A*c9)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos` with t-dependent prefactors. Cannot match.

### 26. `A*c0 + A*c1*log(c2*t + 1) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8 + c9*t) + 1)`
No `sqrt(A)` and no sine term. Cannot match.

### 27. `A*c0 + A*c1/(c2 + t) + c3 + c4*log(c5*(A*c6)**c7 + c8*exp(c9*t) + 1)`
No `sqrt(A)` and no sine term. Cannot match.

### 28. `A*c0 + A*c1/(A + c2) + A*c3/(c4 + t) + c5 + c6*sin(A*c7 + c8)*cos(c9*t)`
This has a `sin(A*c7+c8)` but it is multiplied by `cos(c9 t)`. To remove t-dependence you’d need `c9=0`, making `cos(0)=1`, leaving `c6*sin(A*c7+c8)` (good).
However, there is still **no `sqrt(A)` term**, and the exponential-in-t term `A*exp(-β t)` is also absent. Cannot match.

### 29. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(A*c3) + A*c4/(A + c5) + A*c6/(c7 + t) + c8`
No `sqrt(A)`; has `exp(A*c3)` (wrong dependence; GT has exp in t). Cannot match.

### 30. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3*exp(A*c4) + A*c5/(A + c6) + A*c7/(c8 + t) + c9`
No `sqrt(A)`; wrong exponential dependence. Cannot match.

### 31. `A**2*c0 + A**2*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3*exp(A*c4) + A*c5/(A + c6) + A*c7/(c8 + t) + c9`
No `sqrt(A)`; wrong exponential dependence. Cannot match.

### 32. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8 + c9*t) + 1)`
No `sqrt(A)` and no sine term. Cannot match.

### 33. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)*cos(A*c5) + c6*exp(c7*t)*sin(A*c8 + c9)`
Has a sine term, but multiplied by `exp(c7 t)`; to remove t-dependence set `c7=0`, giving `c6*sin(A*c8+c9)` (good).
Still no `sqrt(A)` term. Also the required `-α A exp(-β t)` could be attempted via the `cos` term? No, it’s `exp(c4 t)*cos(A*c5)` which cannot become `A exp(-β t)` for all A. Cannot match.

### 34. `A*c0 + A*c1/(c2 + t) + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)*cos(A*c9)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 35. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*log(c5*(A*c6)**c7 + c8*exp(c9*t) + 1)`
No `sqrt(A)` and no sine term. Cannot match.

### 36. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*cos(A*c3) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*log(c8*t + 1)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 37. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(c3 + t) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t)*cos(A*c7) + c8*log(c9*t + 1)/A**(1/5)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 38. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3*log(c4*Abs(A) + 1)*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine is in t not in A. Cannot match.

### 39. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(A + c3) + A*c4/(c5 + t) + A*c6*sin(c7*t + c8) + c9`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine is in t not in A. Cannot match.

### 40. `sqrt(A)*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*log(c7*exp(A*c8) + 1)`
Has `sqrt(A)` but multiplied by `exp(c1 t)`; set `c1=0` to get `c0*sqrt(A)` (form ok).
But there is no additive `sin(δA)` term, and no `A*exp(-β t)` term (only `c4*exp(c5 t)` without the leading A). Cannot match.

### 41. `sqrt(A)*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + A*c3 + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*log(c8*exp(A*c9) + 1)`
Again can set `c1=0` to get a plain `sqrt(A)` term.
But still no additive sine term, and the exponential-in-t term is `c5*exp(c6 t)` (missing factor A). Cannot match.

### 42. `A*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*log(c5*exp(A*c6) + 1) + c7*exp(c8*t)*log(A*c9 + 1)`
No `sqrt(A)` and no sine term. Cannot match.

### 43. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + A**c4*c5 + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)*cos(A*c9)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 44. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A**c3*c4 + c5 + c6*exp(c7*t)*cos(A*c8)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 45. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A**c2*c3 + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t)*cos(A*c7) + c8*log(c9*t + 1)/A**(1/5)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 46. `A**(1/3)*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(c3 + t) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*sin(A*c7 + c8*t + c9))`
Has \(A^{1/3}\), not \(\sqrt{A}=A^{1/2}\). No way to change exponent 1/3 to 1/2 (it’s fixed). Also sine is inside exp and depends on t. Cannot match.

### 47. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2/(A + c3) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t)*cos(A*c7) + c8*log(c9*t + 1)/A**(1/5)`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos`. Cannot match.

### 48. `A*c0 + A*c1/(c2 + t) + A*c3 + c4 + c5*exp(c6*sin(A*c7 + c8*t + c9))`
No `sqrt(A)`; sine inside exp and t-dependent. Cannot match.

### 49. `A*c0 + c1 + c2/(c3*exp(c4*t) + 1) + c5*cos(c6*log(c7*Abs(A) + 1) + c8*exp(c9*t))`
No `sqrt(A)`; trig is `cos` of a complicated expression. Cannot match.

### 50. `A**2*c0 + A**2*c1 + A*c2 + c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*sin(A*c7 + c8)*cos(c9*t)`
Has a sine-in-A term multiplied by `cos(c9 t)`; set `c9=0` to remove t-dependence, leaving `c6*sin(A*c7+c8)` (good).
But still no `sqrt(A)` term, and the exponential term is `c4*exp(c5 t)` without the leading `A`. Cannot match.

Across all candidates, none contains **all three** essential GT components in compatible form:
- Only candidates 14, 40, 41 include `sqrt(A)` at all, but none of them has an additive `sin(δA)` term, and none has the required `A*exp(-β t)` structure simultaneously.
- Some candidates include `sin(A*...)` additively (28, 33, 50), but none of those includes `sqrt(A)` and the correct `A*exp(-β t)` term.

Therefore no candidate can be made identical to the GT for all t and A by parameter choice.

GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A*exp(-c2*_s*t) + c3*_p*sin(c4*A)

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.1286*sqrt(A) - 0.1286*A*exp(-0.0594*t) + 0.3894*sin(0.5829*A)`

The GT has three basis functions:
1. `sqrt(A)` — a square root term
2. `A*exp(-αt)` — an exponential decay in t multiplied by A
3. `sin(βA)` — a sine function of A

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

**Key observations about GT structure:**
- Contains `sqrt(A)` (i.e., `A^0.5`)
- Contains `A*exp(c*t)` (linear in A, exponential in t)
- Contains `sin(c*A)` (pure sine of A)
- No constant offset term (though one could be zero)
- No `A²` term, no `A` linear term (unless from Taylor expansion)

Let me check candidates that could potentially match:

**Candidates with `exp(c*sin(...))` terms (1, 3, 4, 9, 10, 11, 12, 13, 46, 48):**
These contain `exp(c*sin(A*c + c))`. This is NOT equivalent to `sin(A*c)` — `exp(sin(...))` is a fundamentally different function from `sin(...)`. These cannot match GT.

**Candidates with `cos(A*c)` but no `sin(A*c)` (2, 5, 25, 33, 34, 37, 43, 44, 45, 47, 50):**
`cos(A*c)` alone cannot produce `sin(A*c)` unless combined with phase shifts. Let me check each.

**Candidate 2:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + Ac2*exp(c3*t) + A^c4*c5 + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)*cos(Ac9)`
- Has `A^c4` which can be `A^0.5 = sqrt(A)` ✓
- Has `A*exp(c3*t)` ✓
- Has `exp(c8*t)*cos(Ac9)` — this couples t and A in the cosine term. GT has `sin(cA)` with no t-dependence. Setting c8=0 gives `cos(Ac9)`, but we need `sin(cA)`. `cos(Ac9)` ≠ `sin(cA)` (they're phase-shifted). But `cos(Ac9)` with c9 chosen appropriately... no, cos and sin differ by a constant phase shift in the argument, not in A's coefficient. Actually, `cos(x) = sin(x + π/2)`, so `cos(cA) = sin(cA + π/2)` which is NOT `sin(cA)`. We need a pure `sin(cA)` term. With c8=0, we get `c7*cos(Ac9)` which cannot equal `sin(cA)`. Also set c0=0 for A², c1=0 for A, c6=0. But we still have cos vs sin mismatch.

Wait — but we also have `c6` as a constant. Could `c6 + c7*cos(Ac9)` somehow produce `sin(cA)`? No, a constant plus cosine cannot equal sine.

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** Similar issue with `cos(Ac9)` coupled with `exp(c8*t)`.

**Candidate 6:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + Ac3*exp(c4*t) + Ac5*log(1+c6/A) + c7 + c8*cos(Ac9)`
- `A*log(1+c6/A)`: For large A this approximates c6, for general A it's not sqrt(A).
- `cos(Ac9)` ≠ `sin(cA)` (phase shift issue — but wait, `cos(x) = sin(x + π/2)`. The argument of cos is `Ac9`, and sin would need `Ac + π/2` which means we'd need `sin(Ac9 + π/2)` = `cos(Ac9)`. So `cos(Ac9)` = `sin(Ac9 + π/2)`. But GT has `sin(0.5829*A)` with no phase offset. So `c8*cos(Ac9)` = `c8*sin(Ac9 + π/2)` ≠ `c8*sin(Ac9)` unless... Actually this IS a valid representation of a sinusoidal function of A. But the GT specifically has `sin(cA)` with no phase shift. `cos(cA)` has a fixed phase shift of π/2. These are different functions.

Actually wait - I need to reconsider. The GT has `sin(c4*A)` where c4 is a specific value. Could `cos(c9*A)` match `sin(c4*A)`? Only if `cos(c9*A) = sin(c4*A)` for all A. This requires `c9*A + π/2 = c4*A + 2πn` for all A, meaning `c9 = c4` and `π/2 = 2πn`, which is impossible. So cos(cA) ≠ sin(c'A) for any constants.
